<td style="line-height:1.3em;">$825.5 million<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mojo_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-Mojo-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></td>
</tr>

<p><i><b>Inception</b></i> is a 2010 <a href="/wiki/Science_fiction_film" title="Science fiction film">science fiction</a> <a href="/wiki/Heist_film" title="Heist film">heist</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thriller_film" title="Thriller film">thriller</a> film written, produced, and directed by <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Nolan" title="Christopher Nolan">Christopher Nolan</a>. The film stars a large ensemble cast that includes <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_DiCaprio" title="Leonardo DiCaprio">Leonardo DiCaprio</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ellen_Page" title="Ellen Page">Ellen Page</a>, <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Gordon-Levitt" title="Joseph Gordon-Levitt">Joseph Gordon-Levitt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marion_Cotillard" title="Marion Cotillard">Marion Cotillard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ken_Watanabe" title="Ken Watanabe">Ken Watanabe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Hardy" title="Tom Hardy">Tom Hardy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dileep_Rao" title="Dileep Rao">Dileep Rao</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cillian_Murphy" title="Cillian Murphy">Cillian Murphy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Berenger" title="Tom Berenger">Tom Berenger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Michael_Caine" title="Michael Caine">Michael Caine</a>. DiCaprio plays a professional thief who commits <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Corporate_espionage" title="Corporate espionage">corporate espionage</a> by infiltrating the subconscious of his targets. He is offered a chance of redemption as payment for a task considered to be impossible: "inception", the implantation of another person's idea into a target's subconscious.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-synop_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-synop-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Shortly after finishing <i><a href="/wiki/Insomnia_(2002_film)" title="Insomnia (2002 film)">Insomnia</a></i> (2002), Nolan wrote an 80-page <a href="/wiki/Film_treatment" title="Film treatment">treatment</a> about "dream stealers" envisioning a <a href="/wiki/Horror_film" title="Horror film">horror film</a> inspired by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lucid_dreaming" title="Lucid dreaming">lucid dreaming</a> and presented the idea to <a href="/wiki/Warner_Bros." title="Warner Bros.">Warner Bros.</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hiscock_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hiscock-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup> Feeling he needed to have more experience with large-scale film production, Nolan retired the project and instead worked on <i><a href="/wiki/Batman_Begins" title="Batman Begins">Batman Begins</a></i> (2005), <i><a href="/wiki/The_Prestige_(film)" title="The Prestige (film)">The Prestige</a></i> (2006), and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Dark_Knight_(film)" title="The Dark Knight (film)">The Dark Knight</a></i> (2008).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Itzkoff_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-Itzkoff-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup> He spent six months revising the script before Warner Bros. purchased it in February 2009.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-first_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-first-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> <i>Inception</i> was filmed in six countries and four continents, beginning in Tokyo on June 19, 2009, and finishing in Canada on November 22, 2009.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-filming_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-filming-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup> Its official budget was US$160 million; a cost which was split between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Warner_Bros" title="Warner Bros">Warner Bros</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Pictures" title="Legendary Pictures">Legendary Pictures</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-budget_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-budget-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup> Nolan's reputation and success with <i>The Dark Knight</i> helped secure the film's $100 million in advertising expenditure.</p>
<p><i>Inception</i> '​s première was held in London on July 8, 2010; its wide release to both conventional and <a href="/wiki/IMAX" title="IMAX">IMAX</a> theaters began on July 16, 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-release_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-release-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup> A box office success, <i>Inception</i> has grossed over $800 million worldwide becoming the <a href="/wiki/List_of_highest-grossing_films" title="List of highest-grossing films">41st-highest-grossing film of all time</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mojo_3-2"><a href="#cite_note-Mojo-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup> The home video market also had strong results, with $68 million in DVD and Blu-ray sales. <i>Inception</i> opened to acclaim from critics, who praised its story, score, and ensemble cast.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Zeitchik_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-Zeitchik-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup> It won four <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Academy_Award" title="Academy Award">Academy Awards</a> for <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Cinematography" title="Academy Award for Best Cinematography">Best Cinematography</a>, <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Sound_Editing" title="Academy Award for Best Sound Editing">Best Sound Editing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Sound" title="Academy Award for Best Sound">Best Sound Mixing</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Visual_Effects" title="Academy Award for Best Visual Effects">Best Visual Effects</a>, and was nominated for four more: <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">Best Picture</a>, <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Original_Score" title="Academy Award for Best Original Score">Best Original Score</a>, <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Production_Design" title="Academy Award for Best Production Design">Best Art Direction</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Writing_(Original_Screenplay)" title="Academy Award for Best Writing (Original Screenplay)">Best Original Screenplay</a>.</p>
<p></p>
